### [219] [An improved PINN framework integrating localized collocation scheme and PIKF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02585)
*Qiang Xi,Wenzhi Xu,Mario Cvetkovic,Dragan Poljak,Timon Rabczuk,Zhuojia Fu*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于局部配点法的物理信息核函数神经网络（LPIKFNN），通过用物理信息核函数（PIKF）和局部配点方案替代自动微分来构建损失函数，有效解决了传统PINN在高阶导数和高波数问题中的计算挑战，并在多个基准问题中验证了其精度和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统PINN在处理高阶导数和高波数问题时面临计算成本高昂的挑战，而现有PIKFNN在处理非均匀问题时存在依赖全局核函数的计算瓶颈。

Method: LPIKFNN引入局部配点方案对局部域内的物理量进行离散化，用PIKF的线性组合表示物理场，训练多层感知机迭代学习物理量；损失函数基于PIKF和局部配点方案构建，而非自动微分，从而避免迭代训练中导数计算的高昂成本。

Result: 通过高波数问题、高阶导数问题、非线性问题、非均匀问题以及基于势的逆肌电图等一系列基准研究，LPIKFNN的数值预测与解析解和实验测量结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: LPIKFNN在计算效率、训练性能和精度上显著优于传统PINN，尤其在高波数和非均匀问题中表现出色，同时消除了PIKFNN对全局核函数的依赖。

Abstract: We propose a localized physics-informed kernel function neural network (LPIKFNN), which is an improved physics-informed neural network (PINN) based on physics-informed kernel function (PIKF). In the LPIKFNN framework, the localized collocation scheme discretizes the physical quantities within the local domain, where the physical field is represented as a linear combination of PIKFs. Based on this representation, the multilayer perceptron is trained to iteratively learn the physical quantities. To overcome the computational challenges of conventional PINN in higher-order derivative and high wavenumber problems, the LPIKFNN constructs the loss function using the PIKF and a localized collocation scheme rather than relying on automatic differentiation. As a result, the costly derivative evaluations required to enforce governing equations during iterative training are eliminated, leading to significantly improved computational efficiency and training performance. Moreover, incorporating PIKFs into the loss function enables the proposed LPIKFNN to significantly improve computational accuracy in high-wavenumber problems characterized by highly oscillatory physical fields. To overcome the computational bottleneck of the physics-informed kernel function neural network (PIKFNN) in heterogeneous problems, the LPIKFNN introduces a localized collocation scheme that removes reliance on global PIKFs, enabling accurate predictions where global PIKFs are unavailable. The feasibility and accuracy of the proposed LPIKFNN are demonstrated through a series of benchmark studies, including high wavenumber problems, higher-order derivative problems, nonlinear problems, heterogeneous problems, and potential-based inverse electromyography. The numerical predictions obtained by LPIKFNN show excellent agreement with available analytical solutions and experimental measurements.

</details>


### [220] [GROSS: German Rail Open-Source SUMO Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03282)
*Juri Penell,Damian Dailisan*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出GROSS，一个结合OpenStreetMap铁路基础设施与GTFS时刻表、面向德国全国范围的开放铁路仿真场景生成管线，可在SUMO中运行。通过拓扑感知的站点映射与分层路由修复，相比传统方法将每车次平均传送（teleportation）减少1.7–76.8倍，并支持生成包含35,925车次的德国全境场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源交通仿真大多面向道路交通，铁路场景缺乏可复现的开放工具链；而现有铁路场景生成方法存在几何匹配不准确、平台/轨道分配不一致等问题，导致仿真中出现路由异常和大量传送伪影，影响仿真稳定性。

Method: GROSS管线包含两个关键步骤：(1) 通过分层车站模型（hierarchical station model）进行拓扑感知的站点映射；(2) 在车站级别进行路由，并配合验证与定向修复（validation and targeted repair）。数据来源为OpenStreetMap铁路基础设施与GTFS时刻表。

Result: 在多个德国区域上，GROSS将每车次平均传送次数降低至原方法的1/1.7–1/76.8，缩短了车辆延误，并能端到端生成包含35,925车次的德国全境场景，与运营商报告的延误统计进行了对比验证。

Conclusion: GROSS降低了构建可扩展、完全开放铁路仿真的门槛，支持国家尺度的延误传播研究；但剩余长延误表明时刻表元数据和铁路调度建模仍存在局限。

Abstract: Microscopic simulation enables reproducible evaluation in intelligent transportation systems, yet most open SUMO scenarios and toolchains remain road-traffic centric, leaving rail underrepresented despite its importance for public transport and its sensitivity to network-wide disruptions. We present the German Rail Open-Source Scenario (GROSS), an open pipeline that combines OpenStreetMap railway infrastructure with GTFS schedules to generate nation-scale rail scenarios for SUMO (Simulation of Urban MObility). Existing conversions often rely on geometry-only stop-to-track matching and inconsistent platform/track assignments, which can create routing anomalies and unstable simulations dominated by teleportation artefacts. GROSS addresses this with topology-aware stop mapping via a hierarchical station model, followed by station-level routing with validation and targeted repair. Across multiple German regions, GROSS reduces average teleportations per vehicle by a factor of 1.7--76.8$\times$, shortens delays compared to the vanilla SUMO pipeline, and it enables end-to-end generation of a Germany-wide scenario with 35\,925 trips for comparisons with operator-reported delay statistics. While the remaining long delays highlight limitations in available timetable metadata and rail dispatch modeling, GROSS lowers the barrier to building scalable, fully open rail simulations and to studying delay propagation at country scale.

### [221] [HonestAffinity: Leak-Aware Evaluation of Protein and Pocket Priors for Binding Affinity Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03422)
*Junhao Wei,Baili Lu,Zhenhong Peng,Wanyan Li,Zhirong Huang,Yanxiao Li,Yifu Zhao,Dexing Yao,Haochen Li,Xudong Ye,Sio-Kei Im,Yapeng Wang,Xu Yang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: HonestAffinity是一个紧凑的1D输入预测器，在无泄漏协议下评估冻结的ESM-2蛋白质嵌入和学习的口袋位置标记两种先验。研究发现，在严格的LP无泄漏测试集上，口袋标记和ESM-2输入反而降低了Pearson R，呈现分裂条件反转现象，而非统一的优先级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于序列的深度学习蛋白质-配体结合亲和力预测方法在标准PDBbind数据划分下会泄露相似性类别，导致评估结果不可靠，且难以解释不同架构先验的真实贡献。

Method: 提出HonestAffinity，一种紧凑的1D输入预测器，使用冻结的ESM-2（650M）蛋白质嵌入和可学习的二进制口袋位置标记作为先验，采用多尺度卷积/Transformer模板，在无泄漏协议下训练于11,513个LP-PDBBind复合物。

Result: 在验证集和CASF-2016上HonestAffinity-Pocket取得最佳平均Pearson R，但在每个严格的LP无泄漏测试集（test_cl1-cl3）上HonestAffinity-Pocket-NoESM取得最佳平均Pearson R。口袋标记和ESM-2在熟悉划分上提升性能，但在严格无泄漏测试集上降低Pearson R。

Conclusion: 模型应报告配对的标准和无泄漏消融实验，部署场景匹配的变体比单一默认模型更能描述这些反转现象。

Abstract: Sequence-based deep learning offers a scalable alternative to structure-based scoring for protein-ligand binding affinity prediction. However, progress is hard to interpret when architectural priors are evaluated on canonical PDBbind-style splits that leak similarity classes across folds. We present HonestAffinity, a compact 1D-input predictor to isolate two priors under a leak-aware protocol: frozen ESM-2 (650M) protein embeddings and a learned binary pocket-position marker. We evaluate a multi-scale convolutional/Transformer template in three variants: HonestAffinity-Pocket, HonestAffinity-NoPocket, and HonestAffinity-Pocket-NoESM. All three train on 11,513 LP-PDBBind complexes in ~3 GPU-hours. We benchmark against five baselines on the LP-PDBBind 3-tier no-leak hold-out, CASF-2016, and a CASF-2016 non-train subset. Our central finding is a split-conditioned reversal rather than a uniformly best prior: HonestAffinity-Pocket achieves the best mean Pearson R on validation and CASF-2016 splits, whereas HonestAffinity-Pocket-NoESM achieves the best mean Pearson R on every strict LP no-leak tier (test_cl1-cl3). Both the pocket marker and ESM-2 input improve performance on familiar splits but reduce Pearson R on strict no-leak tiers. We argue models should report paired canonical and leak-proof ablations, and that deployment-regime-matched variants better describe these reversals than a single default. Code and scripts are linked in the footnote; checkpoints will be released upon acceptance.

### [222] [Physics-Informed Single Atom Matching Pursuit: Guided-Waves Wavenumbers and Propagation Distance Estimation for Damage Localization in Structural Health Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03933)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统导波结构健康监测中，单压电换能器同时激励多个色散导波模态，导致信号解释复杂、损伤监测困难，现有方法缺乏物理可解释性。

Method: 提出PISAMP信号分解方法，将强物理约束（波传播物理原理）嵌入低维、计算高效的信号表示中，直接提取模态波数函数和传播距离等物理意义特征，再结合椭圆定位技术实现损伤定位。

Result: PISAMP能够直接识别关键物理特征（模态波数函数、致动器-损伤-传感器距离），并基于源-损伤-传感器距离利用椭圆定位实现损伤定位。

Conclusion: 将波传播物理集成到紧凑信号分解框架中是本研究的主要创新点，为GW-SHM提供了一种可解释的损伤定位方法。

Abstract: Structural Health Monitoring (SHM) aims at the real-time monitoring of the integrity of engineering structures, with Guided-waves (GWs) providing high sensitivity to damage presence and to ageing effects for thin-walled components. In conventional GW-based SHM, a bonded piezoelectric transducer (PZT) emits a short tone burst that produces an Initial Wave Packet (IWP) propagating through the structure. As this packet interacts with boundaries and potential damages, additional scattered wave packets are produced. A major limitation of such approaches lies in the simultaneous excitation of multiple dispersive GW modes by a single PZT, which significantly complicates signal interpretation and damage monitoring. In this context, this work proposes the Physics-Informed Single Atom Matching Pursuit (PISAMP) method, a signal decomposition method grounded in the physical principles governing wave propagation. In contrast with purely data-driven or numerically intensive techniques, the proposed approach embeds strong physical constraints into a low-dimensional and computationally efficient signal representation. This formulation enables the direct identification of key physically meaningful features, including modal wavenumber functions and propagation distances between actuator, damage and sensors. These extracted features, especially source-damage-sensor distances, allows to subsequently perform damage location using well established Elliptical Localization techniques. The principal novelty of this study lies in integrating wave propagation physics into a compact signal decomposition framework and developing an interpretable damage localization methodology for GW-SHM applications.

### [223] [Samudra 2: Scaling Ocean Emulators across Resolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02610)
*Yuan Yuan,Jesse Rusak,Alexander Merose,Adam Subel,Pavel Perezhogin,Alistair Adcroft,Carlos Fernandez-Granda,Laure Zanna*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: Samudra 2 是一种自回归神经海洋模拟器，通过改进的U-Net架构、ConvNeXt风格模块和动态损失函数，在1°分辨率下将上层海洋温度R²从0.56提升至0.87，将深层海洋温度误差降低约7倍，并能扩展至1/2°和1/4°分辨率进行约8年的自回归滚动模拟，在单个GPU上实现高效运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海洋环流模式（OGCM）计算成本高昂，限制了集合规模和强迫情景数量；现有海洋模拟器未能同时实现高空间分辨率和多年自回归滚动模拟；Samudra存在方差崩溃和印记伪影两种长时程失败模式。

Method: 采用更宽的U-Net主干网络，结合改进的ConvNeXt风格模块并降低模块内部扩展因子；引入动态损失函数，根据预测误差对输出通道重新加权，增强慢演化深层海洋场的梯度信号。

Result: 在1°分辨率下，上层海洋全球平均温度R²从0.56提升至0.87，深层海洋温度误差降低约7倍；可扩展至1/2°和1/4°分辨率实现约8年自回归滚动模拟，恢复中尺度涡旋和强西边界流。

Conclusion: Samudra 2能在单个GPU上实现高效多年代际全球海洋自回归模拟，支持更大规模的海平面预估、海洋热吸收和气候变率研究的集合模拟。

Abstract: Ocean general circulation models (OGCMs) are essential to climate science but computationally expensive, limiting ensemble size and forcing scenarios. Neural emulators promise orders-of-magnitude speedups, yet existing ocean emulators have not combined fine spatial resolution with multi-year autoregressive rollouts. Samudra, the first autoregressive neural ocean emulator to produce multi-decade global rollouts, is limited to $1^\circ$ resolution and exhibits two long-horizon failure modes: \emph{variance collapse}, the loss of temporal variability, and \emph{imprinting artifacts}, in which velocity patterns leak into deep-ocean fields. We present Samudra 2, which introduces a wider U-Net backbone with modified ConvNeXt-style blocks and a reduced block-internal expansion factor, together with a dynamic loss that reweights output channels according to their prediction errors, strengthening gradients for slow-evolving deep-ocean fields. At $1^\circ$, Samudra 2 increases upper-ocean global-mean temperature $R^2$ from 0.56 to 0.87 and reduces deep-ocean temperature error by roughly sevenfold. The same architecture scales to $1/2^\circ$ and $1/4^\circ$ over approximately 8-year autoregressive rollouts, recovering mesoscale eddies and sharp western boundary currents. Running on a single GPU, Samudra 2 enables larger ensembles for sea-level projections, ocean heat uptake, and climate variability studies. We provide code, documentation, and benchmark resources at https://openathena.ai/Ocean_Emulator/.

### [224] [Democracy on Rugged Landscapes: Phase Transitions in Optimal Voting Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02813)
*Joshua Nunley*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文通过NK适应性景观模型，研究了不同投票方法在直接民主与代议民主制度下的表现差异，发现最优投票方法随景观复杂度发生相变，其中波达计数在直接民主的大多数参数空间表现最优，而基数评分投票在代议民主中占主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 法律和制度通过复杂的交互作用影响个体结果，但不同投票方法如何在这种耦合景观中导航尚不明确。本文旨在系统比较多种投票方法在不同复杂度和交叉依赖性条件下的表现。

Method: 将集体治理建模为NK适应性景观上的优化问题，共享位（法律）通过投票更新，个体位（个人特质）固定不变。引入交叉依赖性参数$α$控制法律效果对个人情况的依赖程度。比较了8种标准投票方法和一个广义评分家族，改变景观崎岖度$K$和$α$进行实验。

Result: 直接民主中：基数评分投票在平滑景观占优，序数评分($p=0.35$)在低-中崎岖度最佳，波达计数在中范围占优，STAR投票在最高复杂度最佳。波达计数在大部分参数空间达到最高平均适应度和最低方差。代议民主中：基数评分投票在大多数情况下占主导，高身份权重$β$和低-中候选自利$p_{\mathrm{self}}$条件下，简单多数制（plurality）成为最优方法。

Conclusion: 最优投票方法高度依赖系统的复杂性和交叉依赖性，存在明显的相变现象。波达计数在直接民主中表现稳健，代议民主则重塑了这种复杂度依赖结构。

Abstract: Laws and institutions shape individual outcomes through complex interactions with citizens' diverse circumstances, yet how different voting methods navigate this coupled landscape remains poorly understood. We model collective governance as optimization on NK fitness landscapes, where shared bits (laws) are updated by voting while individual bits (personal traits) remain fixed. A cross-dependency parameter $α$ controls how legislation's effects depend on individual circumstances. We compare eight standard voting methods and a generalized scoring family across landscape ruggedness $K \in \{1,\ldots,20\}$ and $α\in [0,1]$ with 1000 runs per configuration.
  Under direct democracy, the optimal voting method undergoes sharp phase transitions as a function of landscape complexity: cardinal score voting dominates on smooth landscapes, ordinal scoring with $p=0.35$ at low-to-moderate ruggedness, Borda count across a wide middle range, and STAR voting at the highest complexity. A two-parameter empirical formula reduces the $(K, α)$ plane to a single complexity axis for visualization. Borda count achieves the highest mean fitness and lowest variance across most of the parameter space.
  We further introduce a representative democracy model parameterized by identity weight $β$ and candidate self-interest $p_{\mathrm{self}}$. Representation reshapes the complexity-dependent structure even under favorable conditions: cardinal score voting dominates across most regimes, with plurality emerging as the top method at high $β$ and low-to-moderate $p_{\mathrm{self}}$.

Across controlled one-to-one matching environments, mechanism-based markets generally outperform free negotiation in terms of stability and efficiency. We also find that LLM agents report preferences truthfully at substantially higher rates than human subjects in comparable DA and EADA environments. ### [226] [Competitive Information Design in Sequential Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03527)
*Zhicheng Du,Hu Fu,Ying Qin,Zihe Wang*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文在Anderson和Renault(2006)的基础上，将单一广告主-消费者的信息设计模型扩展至水平差异化发送者竞争场景，利用Weitzman指数算法刻画接收者的最优序贯搜索行为，通过对偶方法验证信息策略是否为最佳响应，证明了在先验分布无质量时均衡的存在性，并系统刻画了先验密度单调递增情形下的对称均衡结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将单一广告主的信息披露模型拓展至多发送者竞争环境，研究水平差异化竞争者如何通过战略性信息披露来影响消费者搜索与购买决策。

Method: 采用信息设计框架，基于对偶论证验证信息策略的最佳响应性质，结合Weitzman指数算法刻画消费者序贯搜索行为，分析竞争发送者之间的博弈均衡。

Result: 证明了在先验分布无质量时均衡的存在性，刻画了先验密度单调递增情形下对称均衡的精细结构，并发现均衡可能表现出复杂行为。

Conclusion: 竞争环境下的信息披露均衡具有丰富结构，对偶方法为验证最佳响应提供了有效工具，研究为理解广告竞争中的信息策略提供了理论洞见。

Abstract: Advertisements often strategically disclose information to consumers who make decisions on further information acquisition and eventual purchase. Anderson and Renault (2006) model this problem using an information design framework, where the advertiser acts as a sender and the consumer as a receiver. We extend this model to a competitive setting with horizontally differentiated senders competing for a unit-demand receiver. Under costly inspection, the receiver's optimal sequential search action is given by Weitzman's Index Algorithm.
  We give a method, based on duality arguments, to verify whether a sender's given information strategy constitutes a best response against his competitors (other senders). We establish the existence of an equilibrium in the game among senders when the prior distributions have no mass; we also illustrate that such equilibria may exhibit intricate behaviors. Finally, we meticulously characterize symmetric equilibria played by the senders for cases when the prior distributions have monotone increasing densities, while offering economic intuitions behind the insightful equilibrium structure.

</details>


### [227] [Reserve Depletion and Security Runway in Proof-of-Stake Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03587)
*Paolo Penna,Manvir Schneider*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了权益证明协议中交易费用与代币储备共同资助验证者奖励时的动态过渡问题，通过随机模型推导了维持目标安全水平所需的最小储备阈值，并提供了压力测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 权益证明协议早期交易费用不足以提供足够安全激励，需依赖储备金；后期费用可能充足。核心问题是储备金是否能支撑到费用足够阶段，现有方法（如名义耗尽日期或稳态比率）无法准确评估安全问题。

Method: 建立了离散时间随机模型，包含代币价格和交易需求波动，验证者战略性地选择参与。通过求解验证者进入博弈，推导出状态依赖的储备阈值，将系统分为不可行域、储备依赖安全和费用安全三个区域。进一步扩展至前瞻性验证者，推导马尔可夫参与条件。

Result: 得到了精确的状态依赖储备阈值，将价格和需求的下置信带转化为储备要求的压力测试保证，推导了失败概率和预期过渡时间边界。在扩展模型中获得了前瞻性验证者的马尔可夫参与条件。

Conclusion: 储备政策不应仅依赖名义耗尽日期或稳态奖励比率；协议可能名义储备充足但接近安全失败；一旦需求超过费用阈值，储备对安全不再必要。本文为过渡期压力测试提供了可处理的均衡分析框架。

Abstract: Many proof-of-stake protocols finance validator rewards from two sources: transaction fees and a finite reserve of tokens. This creates a dynamic hand-off problem. Early in the life of the system, fees may be too small to fund the target level of security; later, fees may become sufficient. The central question is whether the reserve provides enough runway for the protocol to remain secure until this fee-only region is reached. We study this problem in a discrete-time stochastic model of validator participation. Token price and transaction demand fluctuate over time, while validators choose participation strategically. We solve the validator entry game and derive an exact state-dependent reserve threshold, i.e., the minimal reserve stock necessary and sufficient to sustain a target security level. This threshold separates three regions: infeasibility, reserve-dependent security, and fee-only security. Security fails if the reserve first falls below the state-dependent threshold, and a successful hand-off occurs exactly if the fee-only region is reached before that failure time. We derive stress-test guarantees that convert lower confidence bands for token price and demand into reserve requirements, and obtain explicit failure-probability and expected hand-off-time bounds. Finally, we extend the model to forward-looking validators and derive the Markov participation condition that captures how current participation affects future reserve-funded rewards. The main implication is that reserve policy should not be evaluated by nominal depletion dates or steady-state reward ratios alone. A protocol can have a large nominal reserve and still be close to security failure after adverse price or demand shocks. Conversely, once demand crosses the fee-only threshold, the reserve becomes redundant for security. This paper provides a tractable equilibrium framework for stress-testing this transition.

</details>


### [228] [Causal Mirage Equilibrium in Agentic Machine Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03636)
*Hamidou Tembine*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出"因果幻象均衡"(CME)概念，形式化描述了生成式机器智能中语义表征与物理现实解耦的稳定化现象，并证明这种解耦不仅是优化异常，而是由递归自回归动力学产生的结构稳定吸引子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统博弈论假设智能体的内部表征与外部状态存在因果联系，但在生成式机器智能中，语义表征可以与物理现实解耦并形成自强化、操作上鲁棒的稳定配置。现有Nash、Bayesian、自我确认或鲁棒均衡等概念无法捕捉这一现象。

Method: 引入风险敏感平均场型博弈框架，定义"因果幻象均衡"(CME)作为精炼解概念；提出无量纲参数"幻象强度"衡量语义脱离程度；利用Kakutani-Glicksberg-Fan不动点定理在联合概率测度空间上证明CME存在性；建立非线性幻象分岔定理。

Result: 当内生强化主导因果根基时，唯一有根基的不动点失稳，产生稳定的非根基状态不变流形；合成共识和因果脱离的语义构型是结构稳定的风险感知吸引子。

Conclusion: 语义脱离现象并非暂时的优化异常，而是递归自回归动力学中结构稳定的均衡现象，需要新的理论框架加以理解和应对。

Abstract: Classical game-theoretic solution concepts assume that agents' internal representations remain causally linked to external states. In generative machine intelligence, this assumption fails: semantic representations can decouple from physical reality, stabilizing into self-reinforcing, operationally robust configurations. This paper introduces the risk-sensitive mean-field-type \emph{Causal Mirage Equilibrium} (CME), a solution refined concept formalizing endogenous epistemic decoupling within a risk-sensitive mean-field-type game. Unlike Nash, Bayesian, self-confirming, or robust equilibria, CME stabilizes detached semantic representation manifolds rather than optimization strategies or observational beliefs. To quantify this phenomenon, we define a dimensionless parameter, the \emph{mirage intensity} which measures semantic detachment as the ratio of an agent's endogenous reinforcement-confidence product to its causally grounded reality alignment. Under compactness, convexity, and continuity assumptions on the game primitives, we prove the existence of an CME using the Kakutani-Glicksberg-Fan fixed-point theorem on the space of joint probability measures. We establish a non-linear mirage bifurcation theorem: when endogenous reinforcement dominates causal grounding, the unique grounded fixed point becomes unstable, giving rise to a stable invariant manifold of ungrounded states. Our results demonstrate that synthetic consensus and causally detached semantic configurations are not transient optimization anomalies, but structurally stable, risk-aware attractors generated by recursive autoregressive dynamics.

### [229] [Fewer, Better Frames: A Compute-Normalized Proof of Concept for Coherence-First World-Model Rendering with Model-Guided FSR4 Frame Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02586)

Abstract: World models are often evaluated by native frame cadence, but higher nominal frame rate can trade away long-horizon scene stability. This article reports an independent proof of concept implemented using Overworld's Waypoint-1.5 family and WorldEngine runtime on a Windows fallback stack with ONNX Runtime + DirectML and an FSR4 DX12 bridge. The tested coherence-first branch generates higher-context anchor frames at a 15 FPS presentation-timeline cadence and reconstructs presentation to 30 FPS using latent-delta motion guidance and synthesized depth. It is compared against a lower-context cadence-first baseline that generates about 30 FPS natively under the same seed, route, control script, target presentation duration, and local time-scaling regime. Across forest, sword, desert, and snow scenes, the coherence-first branch preserves path geometry, object identity, large silhouettes, and depth layering longer, while the baseline degrades earlier into brightness drift and geometric distortion. Lightweight temporal metrics and paired videos support the visual comparison, with LPIPS favoring the coherence-first branch across all tested scenes. Here compute-normalized means approximately matched same-GPU, same-timescale operating points, not exact FLOP parity or measured realtime throughput. A separate heavier sword-scene probe suggests local non-monotonicity: more context and denoising did not automatically improve quality. These results support coherence-first allocation as a practical proof-of-concept strategy under limited inference budget, not as a finished realtime renderer.

Methodology: The method is divided into three main stages: segmentation of the space using Binary Space Partitioning (BSP); logical connection of rooms based on graph traversal to prevent redundant links; and a post-processing stage responsible for cleaning structural artifacts and improving visual cohesion. The methodology allows parameterization of room area and shape, with randomness controlled via seeds for reproducibility. Results: Two experiments were conducted. The first demonstrated the flexibility of the methodology under different seeds and parameter configurations. The second evaluated the navigability of generated maps by verifying connectivity using Breadth-First Search (BFS). ### [231] [PaintBench: Deterministic Evaluation of Precise Visual Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00188)
*Kai Xu,Ellis Brown,Shrikar Madhu,Rob Fergus,He He,Saining Xie*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: PaintBench是一个面向精确视觉编辑的动态可扩展基准测试，涵盖20种基本操作（几何变换、结构操作、颜色变化、符号推理），采用程序化生成和确定性像素级评估。在11个模型中，最高性能仅达17.1%（mIoU），且与下游任务（TinyGrafixBench）评分高度线性相关（R²=0.91）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态模型在开放式视觉编辑上表现良好，但在执行精确的单答案编辑任务时仍存在重要障碍，缺乏系统性的评估基准来衡量这一能力。

Method: 提出PaintBench基准，通过程序化生成方式支持20种精确视觉编辑操作（四类：几何变换、结构操作、颜色变化、符号推理），采用确定性像素级评估指标（mIoU），并构建TinyGrafixBench验证其泛化性。

Result: 11个图像编辑模型中最高分仅17.1%（mIoU）；几何变换、结构操作、公式驱动的颜色变化尤其困难；模型存在特定任务专长分化；场景变化（物体数量、背景复杂度、颜色方案、编辑区域大小）会显著影响性能；PaintBench评分与下游任务评分强线性相关（R²=0.91, p<0.001）。

Conclusion: PaintBench为精确多模态视觉编辑提供了严谨的评估基础，揭示了当前模型在此任务上的严重不足，并为推动该方向进展提供了可靠的度量工具。

Abstract: While current multimodal models are proficient at open-ended visual editing, executing precise single-answer edits remains an important obstacle. To probe this challenge, we introduce PaintBench, a dynamically scalable benchmark targeting 20 fundamental precise visual editing operations across four categories: geometric transformation, structural manipulation, color change, and symbolic reasoning. Procedural generation with configurable complexity enables an effectively infinite, contamination-resistant evaluation suite, and deterministic pixel-level evaluation eliminates reliance on bias-prone judge models. Across 11 image editing models, we find overall low performance, with the current highest-performing industry leader scoring only 17.1% (mIoU). Task decomposition reveals especially challenging operation types (geometric transformation, most structural manipulation, formula-based color change) and model-specific specializations. Fine-grained benchmark diagnostics further show performance degradations induced by scene variations in object count, background complexity, color scheme, and edit-region size. To test generalization of PaintBench scores to applied task performance, we create a procedural, deterministic evaluation for data visualization editing (TinyGrafixBench) and find strong linear correlation with PaintBench scores ($R^2 = 0.91$, $p < 0.001$). Altogether, PaintBench provides a rigorous foundation for measuring and driving progress in precise multimodal visual editing.

### [232] [Reed-Muller type codes over a combinatorial simplex: an algebraic description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02819)
*Hiram H. López,Rodrigo San-José,Nart Shalqini*

TL;DR: 本文利用交换代数工具研究组合单纯形及其关联的CAP码，给出了消没理想的通用Gröbner基，描述了CAP码的广义汉明重量，证明了最小距离的闭式公式，给出了对偶码的生成多项式，并证明了某些情况下CAP码的置换群是对称群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CAP码是Kopparty等人最近提出的高码率Reed-Muller型码，可实现任意高的接近1的码率（对任意固定的最小距离）。本文旨在利用交换代数方法深入分析组合单纯形及其关联的CAP码的结构性质。

Method: 采用交换代数工具，包括Gröbner基、footprint理论、消没理想等，对组合单纯形的代数结构及其CAP码的编码参数进行理论分析。

Result: （1）给出组合单纯形消没理想的通用Gröbner基；（2）用消没理想的footprint描述了CAP码的广义汉明重量；（3）证明了最小距离的闭式公式；（4）给出了生成对偶码的多项式集；（5）描述了保持组合单纯形不变的仿射置换，并证明某些情况下CAP码的置换群是对称群。

Conclusion: 交换代数方法为研究CAP码提供了有效工具，揭示了其代数结构与编码参数之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Given an ordered set $B$ of a finite field, a combinatorial simplex over $B$ is defined as the set of vectors such that the positions of the entries, with respect to $B$, sum up to a fixed integer. CAP codes are Reed-Muller type codes defined over a combinatorial simplex. They were recently introduced by Kopparty et al. as a high-rate alternative to classical Reed-Muller codes, capable of achieving arbitrarily high rates close to one for any fixed minimum distance. In this paper, we use tools from commutative algebra to analyze a combinatorial simplex and its associated CAP code. We give a universal Gröbner basis for the vanishing ideal of a combinatorial simplex. We describe the generalized Hamming weights of a CAP code in terms of the footprint of the vanishing ideal. For the minimum distance case, we proved a closed formula. We give a set of polynomials whose evaluations on the combinatorial simplex generate the dual of the CAP code. We describe the affine permutations that leave invariant a combinatorial simplex and use this information to prove that, in some cases, the permutation group of a CAP code is a symmetric group.

### [233] [Bounds for Single-Error-Correcting Analog Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03011)
*Hengzhuo Li,Hengjia Wei,Xin Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了实数域上模拟码的单纠错问题，证明了冗余度为2的线性码的Γ₂参数下界为1/sin²(π/2n)，解决了Roth的公开问题；同时构造了高冗余度码，得到上界O(n^{1+1/(r-1)})。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Roth提出的关于冗余度为2的单纠错模拟码最优性的公开问题，并推广到更高冗余度情形。

Method: 利用zonotope（带状多面体）的几何特征刻画Γ₂(𝒞)，并引入循环正弦乘积不等式进行下界证明；对于上界，通过构造特定类别的实线性码实现。

Result: 对于任意实线性[n,n-2]码𝒞，Γ₂(𝒞) ≥ 1/sin²(π/2n)；对于固定冗余度r≥2，存在实线性[n,n-r]码使得Γ₂(𝒞) ≤ O(n^{1+1/(r-1)})。

Conclusion: 该下界是最优的，解决了公开问题；高冗余度码的构造为模拟纠错码设计提供了新的上界。

Abstract: We study single-error correction for analog codes over $\mathbb{R}$. A key performance measure is the parameter $Γ_2(\mathcal{C})$, which quantifies the minimum separation required between large outlying errors that need to be located/corrected and bounded tolerable perturbations. We prove that every real linear $[n,n-2]$ code $\mathcal{C}$ satisfies \[ Γ_2(\mathcal{C})\ge \frac{1}{\sin^2(π/2n)}. \] This resolves Roth's open problem on the optimality of redundancy-two single-error-correcting analog codes. Our proof combines a zonotope-based geometric characterization of $Γ_2(\mathcal{C})$ with a cyclic sine-product inequality. We also construct analog codes with higher fixed redundancy and show that, for every fixed $r\ge 2$, there exists a class of real linear $[n,n-r]$ codes such that \[ Γ_2(\mathcal{C})\le O\left(n^{1+\frac{1}{r-1}}\right). \]

</details>


### [234] [Rotatable Antenna Meets Multiple Access: NOMA or OMA?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03035)
*Qi Dai,Beixiong Zheng,Yanhua Tan,Weidong Mei,Jie Tang,Fangjiong Chen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了可旋转天线（RA）辅助通信系统中NOMA与OMA（具体为TDMA）在发射功率最小化方面的性能对比。利用粒子群优化（PSO）算法优化天线旋转角度，结果表明RA方案相比固定天线能显著降低发射功率；在对称用户部署下，RA辅助的NOMA可能不如TDMA，但在非对称场景下NOMA展现出更好的鲁棒性和能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RA技术虽能通过额外空间自由度提升频谱效率，但不同多址接入方案在RA辅助系统下的相对性能优劣尚不明确，亟需理论对比分析。

Method: 采用理论对比方法，在RA辅助通信系统中以发射功率最小化为目标，考虑天线旋转范围和用户目标速率约束，利用PSO算法优化旋转角度，比较NOMA与OMA（TDMA）的性能。

Result: RA方案相比固定天线基准显著降低发射功率；对称部署下RA-NOMA可能劣于TDMA，非对称部署下NOMA具有更好的鲁棒性和能效。

Conclusion: RA技术能有效提升能效，但NOMA与OMA的性能优劣取决于用户部署的对称性：对称场景宜选TDMA，非对称场景宜选NOMA。

Abstract: Rotatable antenna (RA) technology has emerged as a promising solution to enhance spectrum efficiency by exploiting additional spatial degrees of freedom (DoFs) in multiple access networks. However, the relative performance superiority among different multiple access schemes remains largely unclear due to the unique capability of RA in reconfiguring the directional gain pattern. In this letter, we conduct a theoretical comparison between non-orthogonal multiple access (NOMA) and orthogonal multiple access (OMA) schemes in RA-assisted communication systems in terms of transmit power minimization, subject to constraints on antenna rotational range and users' target rates. To address the associated non-convex optimization problem, a particle swarm optimization (PSO) algorithm is employed to optimize the rotational angle. Simulation results demonstrate that RA-assisted schemes significantly reduce transmit power compared to fixed-antenna benchmarks. Furthermore, RA-assisted NOMA may perform worse than time-division multiple access (TDMA) for symmetric user deployments, while it exhibits superior robustness and energy efficiency in asymmetric scenarios.

</details>


### [235] [Classification of independent sets in signed Johnson graphs and applications to kissing arrangements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03299)
*Rustem Takhanov,Stanislav Yun*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了符号Johnson图$J_\pm(n,k)$的最大独立集问题，特别关注$k=4$的情况。开发了适用于$n\le 12$、$n\ne 11$的算法，完整枚举了所有最大独立集（模符号置换同构）。在$n=12$时发现了1579个非同构最大独立集，对应$\mathbb{R}^{12}$中840个点的非等距亲吻排列，展现了该维度下潜在最优亲吻排列的巨大多样性。对于更大$n$，证明了当$n\equiv 2$或$4\pmod{6}$时，所有最大独立集来源于Steiner四元系统，并刻画了非平凡自相容码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号Johnson图是经典Johnson图的重要推广，与常重码理论、极值组合和组合几何密切相关。理解其最大独立集结构对于常数重量码的最优性以及欧氏空间中亲吻数问题有重要意义，尤其是高维空间中潜在最优亲吻排列的多样性尚未被充分探索。

Method: 开发了实用算法，在$n\le 12$、$n\ne 11$范围内模符号置换同构地计算所有最大独立集。结合结构特征刻画，将独立集分类为经典提升（来自最优$(n,4,4)$-码）和非经典构造。对于大$n$，利用组合设计理论建立与Steiner四元系统的联系。

Result: 1) 完成了$n\le 12$（$n\ne 11$）所有最大独立集的枚举与结构刻画；2) 在$n=12$发现1579个非同构最大独立集，其中1575个来自三种不同构造，仅4个为经典提升；3) 证明了$n\equiv 2$或$4\pmod{6}$时最大独立集与Steiner四元系统一一对应；4) 刻画了可构造非经典最大独立集的非平凡自相容码。

Conclusion: 符号Johnson图$J_\pm(n,4)$的最大独立集结构远比经典情况丰富，尤其在$n=12$时展现出惊人的多样性。研究成果为高维空间中最优亲吻排列的探索提供了新的组合视角和分类结果，并建立了与Steiner四元系统等组合设计结构的深层联系。

Abstract: Johnson graph are a family of graphs that play an important role in the theory of constant-weight codes, extremal combinatorics, and combinatorial geometry. We study signed analogues of classical Johnson graphs, denoted by $J_\pm(n,k)$, whose vertices are vectors of the form $\pm e_{i_1}\pm\cdots\pm e_{i_k}$, where two vertices are adjacent whenever their dot product equals $k-1$. We are particularly interested in maximum independent sets in the case $k=4$. An example of such an independent set in $J_\pm(n,4)$, which we call \emph{classical}, is obtained by lifting an arbitrary optimal $(n,4,4)$-code. Such independent sets naturally define kissing arrangements in ${\mathbb R}^n$.
  We develop an algorithm that is practical for computing all maximum independent sets in $J_\pm(n,4)$ up to signed permutations for $n\le 12$, $n\ne 11$. In addition to obtaining complete lists, we provide structural characterizations of all types of maximum independent sets in these dimensions, excluding $n=5$ and $n=11$. Our most striking results concern the case $n=12$. We identify $1579$ non-isomorphic maximum independent sets in $J_\pm(12,4)$, all corresponding to non-isometric kissing arrangements of size $840$ in ${\mathbb R}^{12}$. Structurally, $1575$ of these independent sets arise from three different constructions, the rest are liftings of one of four $(12,4,4)$-codes. To our knowledge, this is the first dimension in which such a large diversity of potentially optimal kissing arrangements has been observed.
  Beyond this finite range, we prove that for $n\equiv 2$ or $4 \pmod 6$, every maximum independent set arises from a Steiner quadruple system. We also obtain a characterization of the so-called \emph{nontrivially self-compatible} codes, namely optimal $(n,4,4)$-codes from which non-classical maximum independent sets can be constructed.

</details>

*Tianrui Qiao,Jun Qian,Ross Murch*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对单射频MIMO-OFDM系统中可重构天线（如ESPAR）引入的模型误差导致的高信噪比下误差平层问题，提出了一种基于马氏距离的最大似然检测方法，有效降低了误码率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单射频MIMO系统使用可重构天线（如ESPAR）时会引入额外的模型误差，导致在高信噪比下出现不可降低的误码率（误差平层），现有检测方法无法有效解决这一问题。

Result: 以ESPAR为例的仿真验证了误差平层分析的正确性，并表明所提增强检测方法能有效解决误差平层问题，在高发射信噪比下显著降低BER。

Abstract: A novel detection method based on maximum-likelihood (ML) detection leveraging Mahalanobis distance is proposed for single-radio-frequency (RF) multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) orthogonal frequency division multiplexing (OFDM) systems. It can enhance bit error rate (BER) performance and is based on the observation that when using reconfigurable antennas (such as electronically steerable parasitic array radiators (ESPARs) to create a single-RF MIMO system, an additional model error arising from the reconfigurable antennas is introduced. These modeling errors produce an irreducible BER (error floor) at high signal-to-noise ratios (SNRs). ### [237] [STC: Reversible Digit-Context Decomposition for BWT-Family Text Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03570)
*Jingyang Du,Yang Shen,Anling Xiang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: STC是一种BWT族压缩器，通过将数字序列与主文本流分离处理，在enwik9上达到157,571,362字节的压缩效果（含解码器），相比未分离的对照版本减少2,629,561字节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BWT类压缩器利用局部上下文规律，但结构化文本中的数字序列（日期、计数器、标识符、坐标等）的变化规律与周围文本不同，现有方法未充分处理这一差异，限制了压缩性能。

Method: 在BWT阶段之前将数字序列从主文本流中分离，用占位符替换主流中的数字序列，将移除的数字按长度和上下文条件存储到侧流中。侧流采用稳定的桶排序和紧凑的数字打包，解码器可从归一化的主流重建原始顺序，无需额外存储排列。各组件由固定的内部BWT/M03风格组件编码器编码。

Result: 在enwik9上，STC生成157,388,188字节的压缩包，加上183,174字节的解码器源码，总计157,571,362字节（LTCB风格）。消融实验表明数字-上下文分解相比未分离对照减少2,629,561字节。结果经完整解码和SHA-256验证。

Conclusion: 分离数字序列的上下文处理能有效提升BWT类压缩器对结构化文本的压缩性能，该方法已在enwik9上验证有效，但官方基准状态需独立维护方验证。

Abstract: Burrows-Wheeler-transform-based compressors rely on local context regularity, but structured text also contains dates, counters, identifiers, coordinates, and other digit runs whose values vary differently from their surrounding tokens. STC is a practical BWT-family compressor that separates this source of variation before the component BWT stage. It replaces digit runs in the main stream with an unambiguous placeholder and stores the removed digits in length- and context-conditioned side streams. The side streams use stable bucket ordering and compact digit packing, so the decoder can reconstruct the original run order from the normalized main stream without storing a separate permutation. The resulting components are encoded by a fixed internal BWT/M03-style component coder. On enwik9, STC produces a 157,388,188-byte archive with a 183,174-byte decoder source package, giving a local LTCB-style total of 157,571,362 bytes. A full-enwik9 same-coder ablation shows that the digit-context decomposition reduces the archive by 2,629,561 bytes relative to the no-split control. The result is locally verified by full decode and SHA-256 matching; official benchmark status requires independent maintainer-side verification.

### [238] [Finite-Temperature de Bruijn Identities: Fisher Information as the Spectral Gap of Blahut--Arimoto Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03813)
*Qiao Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文发现了一个有限温度版本的de Bruijn恒等式，将Blahut-Arimoto动力学谱隙与Fisher信息联系起来。经典de Bruijn恒等式是该恒等式在β→∞时的极限情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典de Bruijn恒等式连接微分熵与Fisher信息，但仅适用于高斯卷积的极限情形。作者希望建立有限温度下的精确对应关系，揭示其与率失真优化中BA谱理论的深层结构关联。

Method: 利用Blahut-Arimoto动力学的谱理论，分析高斯信源下BA松弛核的谱隙λ = 1/(2βσ²)，并与Fisher信息J = 1/σ²对比，建立λ = J/(2β)的关系，进而推导BA自由能F_β关于σ²的偏导恒等式。

Result: 得到了精确的有限温度de Bruijn恒等式：∂F_β/∂σ² = 1/(2βσ²) = λ，该等式对所有有限β成立。经典de Bruijn恒等式β·∂F_β/∂σ² = J/2作为β→∞的极限情形自然导出。

Conclusion: 经典de Bruijn恒等式并非孤立事实，而是率失真优化谱几何中一族精确恒等式的β→∞极限。该发现对熵幂不等式、BA动力学的χ²-耗散结构以及信息不等式的几何统一有重要启示。

Abstract: We uncover a finite-temperature extension of de Bruijn's identity -- the classical relation $\frac{d}{dt}h(X+\sqrt{t}Z)=\frac{1}{2}J(X)$ connecting differential entropy and Fisher information. Our framework is the spectral theory of Blahut--Arimoto (BA) dynamics, recently developed by Wang~\cite{Wang2026} for the analysis of rate-distortion optimization.
  The central observation is elementary yet profound: for Gaussian sources, the spectral gap $\lam$ of the BA relaxation kernel $\G$ satisfies $\lam = 1/(2βσ^2)$~\cite{Wang2026}, while the Fisher information of the source is $J = 1/σ^2$. Hence \[ {\lam = \frac{J}{2β}} \] for all inverse temperatures $β> 1/(2σ^2)$. This identifies the BA spectral gap as a \emph{finite-temperature regularization of Fisher information}.
  From this observation we derive an exact finite-temperature de Bruijn identity: \[ \frac{\partial F_β}{\partial σ^2} = \frac{1}{2βσ^2} = \lam, \] where $F_β$ is the BA free energy. This identity holds for all finite $β$ without any limit procedure. The classical de Bruijn identity follows as the exact consequence $β\,\partial F_β/\partialσ^2 = J/2$.
  The significance is structural: classical de Bruijn is not an isolated fact about Gaussian convolutions, but the $β\to\infty$ shadow of a one-parameter family of exact identities living in the spectral geometry of rate-distortion optimization. We discuss implications for the entropy power inequality, the $χ^2$-dissipation structure of BA dynamics, and the geometric unification of information inequalities.

</details>


### [239] [Sparse Activation for Sustainable Cell-Free Massive MIMO Networks: Less is More](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03912)
*Zhe Wang,Shuaifei Chen,Emil Björnson*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对6G可持续网络愿景，研究了无蜂窝大规模MIMO网络中的稀疏天线/阵列激活问题。提出了一种天线级最优双线性均衡器（OBE）加权框架，将传统大尺度衰落解码（LSFD）从标量系数推广为天线单元感知的矩阵加权。在此基础上，通过结构化稀疏诱导的均方误差最小化问题，设计了天线级和阵列级两种粒度的激活方案，每种方案包含UE特定和全网两种变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现第六代（6G）网络的可持续性，通过稀疏天线/阵列激活降低无蜂窝大规模MIMO网络的能耗。

Method: 1. 提出天线级最优双线性均衡器（OBE）加权框架，为每个AP-UE对分配矩阵值长期权重；2. 将稀疏天线激活建模为结构化稀疏诱导的MSE最小化问题；3. 设计四种激活方案（天线级/阵列级 × UE特定/全网）；4. 采用近端方法和树结构近端算子求解凸优化问题。

Result: OBE加权方案持续提升频谱效率，且增益随天线数增加而增大；所提稀疏激活方案能在可控制的频谱效率损失下实现显著的能效提升和功耗降低。

Conclusion: OBE框架和稀疏激活方案为6G可持续无蜂窝大规模MIMO网络提供了有效的能效优化手段，在频谱效率与能耗之间实现了良好的折中。

Abstract: Motivated by the vision of making sixth-generation (6G) networks sustainable, we study the sparse antenna/array activation problems in uplink cell-free massive multiple-input multiple-output (CF mMIMO) networks. We first develop an antenna-level optimal bilinear equalizer (OBE) weighting framework, in which each access point-user equipment (AP-UE) pair is assigned a matrix-valued long-term weight to shape the contribution of individual antenna elements, thereby generalizing the conventional large-scale fading decoding (LSFD) strategy from scalar coefficients to antenna-element-aware weighting. Building on this structure, we formulate sparse antenna activation as structured sparsity-inducing mean square error (MSE) minimization problems, and design four activation schemes at two granularities: antenna-level and array-level, each with UE-specific and network-wide (all-UEs) variants. The resulting convex problems are solved efficiently via the proximal method with closed-form group-wise updates, while the network-wide schemes are modeled through hierarchical sparsity and handled by a tree-structured proximal operator. Numerical results under correlated Rician channels and a detailed power consumption model demonstrate that the OBE weighting scheme consistently improves spectral efficiency over the LSFD, with gains increasing with the number of antennas. Meanwhile, the studied sparse activation schemes can achieve substantial energy efficiency improvement and power reduction with controllable spectral efficiency loss.

### [240] [Visual Graph Scaffolds for Structural Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02673)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Graphs have been used to enhance large language models (LLMs) for structured reasoning, mostly as external knowledge sources are provided to models at test time. In this paper, we take a different view: the value of graphs for LLMs lie not only in supplying information, but also in organizing reasoning. Inspired by how humans use graph-structured mind maps to organize branching and converging thoughts, we ask whether graphs can serve as an internal form of reasoning assistance. We study this question on multi-hop question answering tasks, where teacher-provided reasoning traces are rewritten as graph mind maps and used to guide a student model. Our experiments reveal a clear modality gap. When graph structures are flattened into text, their benefits become limited once direct answer hints are removed. Under this abstract guidance setting, both reasoning efficiency and answer quality degrade substantially. In contrast, visual graph guidance remains effective without direct answer clues, and its advantage persists after supervised fine-tuning and KL-based distillation. The above findings support the claim that graphs should be studied not only as external knowledge structures for LLMs, but also as visual scaffolds for organizing reasoning.

### [241] [AURA: Action-Gated Memory for Robot Policies at Constant VRAM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02775)
*Josef Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AURA-Mem提出了一种适用于机器人场景的恒定大小循环记忆架构，通过动作效用门控机制决定何时写入记忆，在保持与KV-cache相当性能的同时，将写入次数减少5-9倍，记忆大小固定为4,224字节，适用于资源受限的边缘设备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据中心推理场景与机器人具身智能场景存在根本差异：数据中心可批量处理短请求并重置KV-cache，而机器人设备在带宽受限的边缘硬件上运行单一、不重置的长程episode，高带宽内存和闪存稀缺，闪存写入寿命有限，内存写入而非计算成为约束瓶颈。现有KV-cache在此场景下会无限增长。

Method: 在冻结的视觉-语言-动作骨干网络外围包裹一个恒定大小的循环记忆模块和一个可学习的门控机制，该门控仅在当前观测会改变下一步动作时才执行写入操作（即"知道何时保持沉默的记忆"）。与基于重建的信号不同，门控直接通过闭环动作误差信号进行训练。

Result: 在合成基准测试中，AURA-Mem在准确率上与最优O(1)基线持平，同时写入次数减少5.19-6.13倍（简单配置下最高减少9.19倍）。在LIBERO-Long的OpenVLA-OFT 7B策略评估中，AURA-Mem成功率达到0.233（与无门控基线持平），优于始终写入的KV基线（0.217），写入次数减少7.0倍且记忆大小恒定。

Conclusion: AURA-Mem证明了在机器人具身智能场景下，基于动作效用信号的门控循环记忆能够在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅减少内存写入次数和占用空间，是KV-cache在边缘设备上的有效替代方案。

Abstract: The KV-cache is the right memory for datacenters but the wrong memory for robots. Datacenter inference batches many short requests and resets them, amortizing an attention cache across a crowd. Embodied agents instead run one long, non-resetting episode on bandwidth-limited edge hardware, where high-bandwidth memory and flash are scarce, flash has finite write endurance, and memory writes rather than compute can become the binding constraint.
  AURA-Mem (Action-Utility Recurrent Adaptive Memory) targets this regime. It wraps a frozen vision-language-action backbone with a constant-size recurrent memory and a learned gate that writes only when the current observation would change the next action: memory that knows when to stay silent. Unlike reconstruction-based memory, the gate is trained directly against a closed-loop action-error signal. Its inference state is fixed at 4,224 bytes regardless of horizon, while a KV-cache grows to 6,061 times larger at 100,000 steps.
  On a controlled synthetic benchmark, AURA-Mem matches the best O(1) baseline in accuracy while using 5.19-6.13 times fewer writes, and up to 9.19 times fewer writes on easier configurations. Budget-matched random and periodic schedules do not recover this gain, isolating the benefit to the action-surprise signal. On a trained closed-loop OpenVLA-OFT 7B panel on LIBERO-Long (n=60 episodes per arm), the gate does not hurt success: AURA-Mem matches the ungated base policy (0.233) and slightly exceeds an always-write KV arm (0.217), while using 7.0 times fewer writes and constant memory. We also instantiate an approximate-information-state value-loss bound as a methodology demonstration; at this scale, the bound is vacuous rather than a guarantee.

</details>


### [242] [Evaluating Transformer and LSTM Frameworks for Prediction in Ungauged Basins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02791)
*Taye Akinrele,James Halgren,Noorbakhsh Amiri Golilarz,Sudip Mittal,Shahram Rahimi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究比较了仅编码器Transformer和LSTM在无观测流域上游流量推断中的表现，发现LSTM整体优于Transformer，而加入下游信息可使模型性能提升60%以上。作者认为这反映了循环记忆架构更适合水文序列推断任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无观测流域中，缺乏直接观测数据增加了不确定性并限制了对极端事件的预测能力。评估更优的深度学习架构（如Transformer vs LSTM）对于上游径流推断具有重要意义。

Method: 使用NOAA国家水文模型（NWM）的回顾性模拟数据，比较仅编码器Transformer与LSTM在仅有上游信息及结合上下游信息两种配置下的上游径流推断性能。

Conclusion: 循环记忆（LSTM）相比仅编码器Transformer更适合上游径流重建任务，而下游水文背景信息作为强辅助约束能显著提升跨架构的预测能力。

Abstract: Watershed networks exhibit convergent topologies in which multiple tributaries merge into downstream channels,integrating diverse upstream hydrological processes. In ungauged basins, the absence of direct observations increases uncertainty and limits the ability to anticipate extreme events. This study evaluates whether an encoder-only Transformer provides an advantage over an LSTM for upstream streamflow inference under limited hydrologic information, using retrospective simulations from the NOAA National Water Model (NWM). Across both upstream-only and combined configurations, the LSTM showed stronger overall performance than the Transformer model across the two configurations. Incorporating downstream information further boosted performance for all models, increasing median NNSE by more than 60%. Rather than treating this as a leaderboard-style comparison, we interpret the experiments as a test of architectural inductive bias for hydrologic sequence inference. The results indicate that recurrent memory remains better aligned with this upstream reconstruction task than an encoder-only Transformer, while downstream hydrologic context provides a strong auxiliary constraint that substantially improves prediction skill across architectures

### [245] [Traj-Evolve: A Self-Evolving Multi-Agent System for Patient Trajectory Modeling in Lung Cancer Early Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02812)
*Sihang Zeng,Matthew Thompson,Ruth Etzioni,Meliha Yetisgen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Traj-Evolve，一个结合经验池（非参数记忆，存储拒绝采样推理轨迹）和多智能体强化学习（参数优化）的自我进化多智能体系统，通过留一交叉检索策略统一训练和推理，在肺癌预测任务上优于9个强基线模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 经验池(ExPool)：非参数记忆，存储拒绝采样的推理轨迹，检索相似患者作为少样本上下文；(2) 多智能体强化学习(MARL)：通过奖励排序微调参数化优化智能体间及智能体-记忆协作；(3) 留一交叉检索策略统一训练和推理阶段。

Result: 在利用长达五年多模态EHR数据的肺癌预测任务上，Traj-Evolve在整体人群和具有挑战性的从不吸烟人群中均优于9个强基线模型。

Abstract: Modeling patient trajectories from longitudinal electronic health records (EHRs) requires reasoning over sparse, noisy, and long-context multimodal sequences. Existing LLM-based multi-agent systems address context length but process patients in isolation, failing to mirror how clinicians leverage accumulated experience from similar prior cases. We present Traj-Evolve, a self-evolving multi-agent system with two complementary evolving mechanisms. First, an Experience Pool (ExPool) acts as a non-parametric memory, indexing rejection-sampled reasoning traces to retrieve similar patients as few-shot contexts. Second, multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) via reward-ranked fine-tuning parametrically optimizes inter-agent and agent-memory collaboration. A leave-one-out cross-retrieval strategy unifies the two, aligning training- and inference-time behavior under retrieval augmentation. On a lung cancer prediction task utilizing up to five years of multimodal EHRs, Traj-Evolve outperforms 9 strong baselines on the overall population and a challenging never-smoker population. Analysis of the evolving dynamics highlights three key findings: (1) expanding the ExPool shifts optimal retrieval from diverse to specific samples; (2) under MARL, the manager agent's prediction loss converges quickly while the worker agents' temporal reasoning continues to benefit from more verified patients; and (3) the two mechanisms are complementary on the predicted risk, where ExPool improves specificity while MARL improves sensitivity.

### [247] [Thinking Past the Answer: Evaluating Harmful Overthinking in Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02835)
*Simone Caldarella,Davide Talon,Rahaf Aljundi,Elisa Ricci,Massimiliano Mancini*

TL;DR: 本文发现大型推理模型在获得正确答案后继续推理会导致有害的过度思考，通过引入前缀级轨迹评估协议，证明在首次正确前缀处停止可将准确率提升最高21%，揭示了模型不仅受限于推理能力，更受限于"不知道何时停止"的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑"更长推理始终有益"的假设，探究模型在获得正确答案后的进一步推理是精化解还是偏离正确答案。

Method: 提出前缀级轨迹评估协议，基于推理充分性定义最小推理预算，区分冗余无害的冗长过度思考和破坏正确轨迹的有害过度思考。

Result: 多模态基准测试表明许多被认为需要大量推理的实例实际所需推理很少；在首次正确前缀处停止相比标准推理提升准确率最高达21%；早停策略可减少50%冗长过度思考但无法缓解有害过度思考；错误主要由逻辑漂移和视觉重新解释导致。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) improve performance by generating explicit intermediate reasoning traces through increased test-time compute, yet the assumption that longer reasoning is consistently beneficial remains under-examined. While recent evidence shows that additional reasoning can lead models to overthink, we ask: "Once a model has reached the correct answer, does further reasoning refine the solution, or deviate from it?" To study the dynamics after correctness, we introduce a prefix-level trajectory evaluation protocol grounded in reasoning sufficiency, defining the minimum reasoning budget required for a model to first generate the correct answer. This allows us to disentangle verbose overthinking, where additional reasoning is redundant but harmless, from harmful overthinking, where continued reasoning destabilizes an already-correct trajectory. Starting from multimodal benchmarks, we find that many instances considered reasoning-intensive require surprisingly little reasoning. Moreover, stopping at the first correct prefix improves accuracy over standard reasoning up to 21%, revealing that current models are limited not only by their ability to reason, but also by their inability to stop at the right time. Furthermore, while common efficiency strategies like early stopping substantially reduce verbose overthinking (up to 50%), they fail to mitigate harmful overthinking. Failure analysis reveals that correctness deviations are mainly driven by logical drift and visual reinterpretation. Finally, we show that our findings generalize to language-only reasoning benchmarks, highlighting harmful overthinking as a broader reliability risk. Code available at https://simonecaldarella.github.io/thinking-past-the-answer.

### [249] [Don't Gamble, GAMBLe: An Analytical Framework for AI-Driven Research Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02863)
*Marquita Ellis,Paul Castro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出GAMBLe框架，将AI驱动研究系统（ADRS）分解为四个参数（生成器G、评估器A、发现机制M、预算B）和一个组合对象（有效景观L_eff），并通过760+次实验（>46,000次迭代）发现：组件间无全序关系，前沿模型可能不如开源方案，简单机制有时超越复杂元搜索，合适组件选择可在有限预算下提升13-67%性能并提高6-39倍搜索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ADRS性能依赖组件间相互作用，但这些相互作用理解不足、探索成本高，且标准收敛保证无法有效刻画ADRS过程，因此需要新的分析框架。

Method: 提出GAMBLe框架，将ADRS行为分解为生成器G、评估器A、发现机制M、预算B四个参数，以及有效景观L_eff = A ∘ G这一组合对象，并在三个NP难问题上进行760+次复现实验（>46,000次迭代）。

Result: 1）不存在生成器或发现机制的全局最优排序；2）前沿模型可能不如开源方案；3）简单贪婪机制有时超越最先进的协进化元搜索；4）在60次迭代的有限预算下，合适的组件选择可提升13-67%性能和6-39倍搜索效率。

Conclusion: ADRS的性能高度依赖于组件间的具体组合，而非单个组件的绝对优势；GAMBLe框架为理解和优化ADRS提供了有效的分析工具。

Abstract: AI-Driven Research Systems (ADRS) -- systems coupling LLMs with automated evaluation to discover algorithms, proofs, and designs -- are being optimized and adopted across domains, but the tools to analyze them have not kept pace. ADRS performance depends on component interactions that are poorly understood, expensive to explore, and (as we show) not well captured by standard convergence guarantees. These guarantees rely on structural assumptions that do not hold under the ADRS process we formalize. We introduce GAMBLe, a framework that decomposes ADRS behavior into four parameters (generator $G$, assessor $\mathcal{A}$, discovery mechanism $\mathcal{M}$, budget $B$) and one compositional object, the effective landscape $L_{\text{eff}} = \mathcal{A} \circ G$, which reveals that distinct generator-assessor pairs induce structurally different per-problem optimization landscapes. We exercise the framework on 760+ replicated runs (>46,000 iterations) spanning generators from single LLMs to dynamically-adaptive ensembles, mechanisms from greedy selection to co-evolutionary meta-search, and three NP-hard problems whose assessors range from continuous scoring to cliff functions. The experiments reveal no total ordering of generators or mechanisms: frontier models can underperform open-source alternatives and the simplest mechanism sometimes outperforms state-of-the-art meta-search. Results show that even under limited budgets (60 iterations per run), the right component choices can improve performance by 13-67% and search efficiency by 6-39x.

### [250] [When Helping Hurts and How to Fix It: Multi-Agent Debate for Data Cleaning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02866)
*Chirag Parmar,Akshat Mehta,Henglin Wu,Jagadish Ramamurthy,Shweta Medhekar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 多智能体辩论对数据清洗的影响具有双重性：在生成任务中由于"批评诱导混淆"(CIC)现象导致性能下降1.6-15.5个百分点，但在错误检测上提升27.4个F1点。研究发现辩论有效的条件是"拯救错误输出的概率大于破坏正确输出的概率"，并通过对抗性分离（独立的Critic+代码执行+证据门控生成）首次在生成任务上显著超越单智能体（+5.3pp）。该条件在9种任务类型和19项已发表比较中零误报地泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究多智能体辩论在数据清洗场景下何时有效、何时有害，并建立可预测辩论效果的理论条件。

Method: 在3个基准、4个模型家族、6000+任务-条件对上系统评估辩论效果；提出"辩论收益条件"（辩论有益当拯救错误输出的概率大于破坏正确输出的概率）；设计因子实验验证对抗性分离（独立Critic+代码执行基础+证据门控生成）的必要性。

Result: 辩论在生成任务上导致-1.6到-15.5pp的性能下降（归因于CIC现象），但在错误检测上提升27.4 F1（d=1.0）。对抗性分离配置首次在生成任务上超过单智能体（+5.3pp, p<0.05）。辩论收益条件在9种任务类型和19项已发表比较中零误报泛化。

Conclusion: 多智能体辩论并非普遍有益，其效果取决于任务类型和架构设计。对抗性分离（包括独立Critic、代码执行基础、证据门控生成）是实现辩论收益的关键，且提出的辩论收益条件能有效预测何时辩论会有帮助。

Abstract: When does multi-agent debate help data cleaning, and when does it hurt? Across three benchmarks, four model families, and over 6,000 task-condition pairs, we find debate's effect reverses sign: it degrades generation across all four models (-1.6 to -15.5pp) through critique-induced confusion (CIC), hallucinated Critic feedback that the Generator accepts uncritically, yet improves error detection (+27.4pp F1, d=1.0). We derive a debate benefit condition: debate helps when the probability of rescuing a wrong output (Critic verification odds weighted by fixability) exceeds the probability of destroying a correct one. A factorial experiment proves adversarial separation is essential: self-verification with identical tools fails, while a separate Critic with code-execution grounding and evidence-gated generation produces the first debate configuration to significantly exceed single-agent on a generative task (+5.3pp, p<0.05). The condition correctly predicts all nine task types and generalizes with zero false positives across 19 published comparisons in seven domains.

TL;DR: 本文提出"交接债务"概念，通过中断协议模拟代码代理被中断后由后继代理接管的场景，发现上下文交接（如原始轨迹、摘要笔记）相比仅仓库状态接管可显著减少代理事件和提示词消耗，但解决率影响较小且依赖模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码代理评测仅关注单个代理不间断完成任务，但现实软件任务常被中断、重新分配或交接给其他代理/工程师，缺乏对交接成本的量化评估。

Method: 设计接管协议：在确定性交接点中断代码代理，冻结仓库状态，让后继代理在四种交接视图（仅仓库状态、原始轨迹、摘要笔记、结构化笔记）下恢复任务。基于75个源任务生成181个交接点任务和每个后继模型724次接管运行。

Result: 相比仅仓库状态接管，上下文交接在三个后继模型上中位代理事件减少20-59%，累积提示词减少42-63%；解决率改善较小且依赖具体模型，但效率提升一致。

Conclusion: 代码代理评测不仅应报告是否解决了任务，还应报告另一个代理恢复该工作的成本。

Abstract: Coding-agent benchmarks evaluate whether a single uninterrupted agent can resolve a repository issue. Real software work is messier: tasks are interrupted, reassigned, reviewed, and resumed from partial states left by another agent or engineer. We study this missing dimension through \emph{handoff debt}: the rediscovery cost imposed when a predecessor's work is opaque or incomplete. Our takeover protocol interrupts a coding agent at deterministic handoff points, freezes the repository, and evaluates successor agents under four handoff views: repository state only, raw trace, summary notes, and structured notes. Across 75 source tasks, the protocol generates 181 handoff-point tasks and 724 takeover runs per successor model. Across three successor models, context-bearing handoffs reduce median agent events by 20--59\% and cumulative prompt tokens by 42--63\% relative to repository-only takeover. Solved-rate effects are smaller and model-dependent, but efficiency gains are consistent. These findings suggest that coding-agent evaluation should report not only whether a task is solved, but also how costly that work is for another agent to resume.

</details>

Abstract: Background: Oral diseases affect nearly 3.5 billion people worldwide, yet the comparative clinical potential of large-scale AI models in dentistry remains poorly understood. Three distinct model categories have emerged: language-generative models, discriminative vision foundation models, and dental-specific foundation models, with no unified review examining their relationships and collective limitations.
  Methods: Following PRISMA-ScR guidelines, we systematically searched four databases (PubMed, Google Scholar, Scopus, arXiv), screened independently by two reviewers. After applying inclusion/exclusion criteria, 97 studies (2020-2026) were included. We propose a two-dimensional classification framework organizing models by architectural paradigm and dental specialization degree.
  Results: Language-generative models excel at text-based tasks (clinical reasoning, licensing exams, patient communication) but show inconsistent performance on image-dependent diagnostics. Adapted SAM and CLIP variants achieve strong tooth segmentation and lesion detection results. Dental-specific models (DentVFM, DentVLM, OralGPT) demonstrate strongest performance on complex multimodal tasks. Integrated pipelines consistently outperform single-model approaches. A data asymmetry is observed: dental-specific pretraining concentrates almost entirely in the vision domain, reflecting scarce large-scale dental text corpora.
  Conclusions: General-purpose and dental-specific models play complementary roles; the most effective systems combine both within structured pipelines. ### [253] [What Benchmarks Don't Measure: The Case for Evaluating Abstention Competence in Autonomous Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02965)
*Victor Ojewale,Suresh Venkatasubramanian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了自主智能体系统中存在“顺从偏差”（compliance bias）问题——智能体在缺乏必要输入、证据或授权时仍倾向于执行操作，而非安全地暂停。作者提出三缺口分类法（规范缺口、验证缺口、权限缺口），并引入三种评估协议（安全率、可用率、知情拒绝率），实验表明运行时强制的中止机制可在不同模型家族中实现可调的安全-可用性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主智能体基准测试仅关注任务完成与否，但系统性地忽略了智能体是否应当执行该任务的问题。人类反馈训练框架下的智能体存在结构性倾向：即使缺乏安全行动的前提条件（输入、证据或授权），仍然选择继续执行，这种“顺从偏差”源于奖励信号和基准评分机制都将“继续执行”视为默认正确行为。

Method: 1. 理论溯源：证明顺从偏差源自人类反馈管道中的奖励破解（reward hacking），并被现有智能体基准测试所固化（要么惩罚暂停行为，要么架构上无法区分原则性暂停与静默失败）。2. 分类框架：提出三缺口分类法——规范缺口（所需信息缺失）、验证缺口（世界状态无法确认）、权限缺口（未获得明确授权）。3. 评估协议：提出安全率（Safety Rate）、可用率（Usability Rate）、知情拒绝率（Informed Refusal Rate）三项指标。4. 实验验证：在144个企业智能体场景和5个模型家族上测试运行时强制中止机制的效果。

Result: 运行时强制的中止机制能够实现高达89.2%的危险行为阻断率、87.5%的授权场景可用率。安全-可用性权衡是可调的而非固有的，且其形态在不同模型家族间差异显著。

Conclusion: 顺从偏差是自主智能体安全部署中的关键未解决问题，本文提出的分类法和复合指标可作为后续研究的起点，表明在保证安全的同时维持可用性是可以通过可调机制实现的。

Abstract: Benchmarks for autonomous agents measure whether agents complete tasks, yet this framing is systematically blind to whether an agent should have proceeded at all. Agents trained under human-feedback objectives develop a structural tendency to proceed even when they lack the inputs, evidence, or authorization to act safely, a disposition we term compliance bias, because both the reward signal and the benchmark scoring regime treat proceeding as the correct default regardless of whether the preconditions for safe action are present. We make three contributions. We first show that compliance bias originates in reward hacking within human-feedback pipelines and is entrenched by prominent agent benchmarks, which either penalize agents for pausing or are architecturally unable to distinguish a principled pause from a silent failure. We then introduce a three-gap taxonomy of abstention-warranted scenarios, covering specification gaps where required information is absent, verification gaps where world state cannot be confirmed, and authority gaps where explicit authorization has not been given, which together provide a principled basis for constructing abstention-aware agent benchmarks. Finally, we propose abstention evaluation protocols (Safety Rate, Usability Rate, and Informed Refusal Rate) and report preliminary results across 144 enterprise agent scenarios and five model families, in which a runtime-enforced abstention mechanism achieves up to 89.2% hazardous-action blocking and 87.5% usability on authorized scenarios, demonstrating that the safety--usability tradeoff is tunable rather than inherent and that its shape varies substantially across model families. We treat this as preliminary work and offer the taxonomy and composite metrics as a starting point for further conversations.

</details>

Abstract: Human Activity Recognition (HAR) using WiFi signals has emerged as a transformative technology for smart homes, healthcare monitoring, security systems, and ambient assisted living. Unlike traditional camera-based systems that raise significant privacy concerns and fail in low-light conditions, or wearable sensors that require user compliance, WiFi-based HAR is non-intrusive, privacy-preserving, cost-effective, and works seamlessly in any lighting condition. This paper presents a comprehensive approach to recognize three distinct human activities: "No Presence" (empty room), "Walking", and "Walking + Arm-waving" using the Wallhack1.8k WiFi spectrogram dataset. We propose three key improvements to address the main challenges in WiFi-based HAR. First, to address high performance variance, we implement ensemble learning with five different CNN architectures (Deep CNN, Wide CNN, MobileNetV2, ResNet50V2, and EfficientNetB0). Second, to address the small dataset size limitation, we apply aggressive data augmentation techniques including time-warping, frequency masking, and noise addition. Third, to evaluate real-world generalization capability, we perform cross-scenario evaluation (training on Line-of-Sight and testing on Non-Line-of-Sight) and cross-antenna evaluation (training on Biquad antenna and testing on PIFA antenna). Our ensemble model achieved a test accuracy of 94.87% on the LOS scenario with Biquad antenna, outperforming the best individual model by 0.66%. *Zhihan Lei,Jiarui Yan,Joshua Momo,William W. Cohen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出推理基元归纳法（Reasoning Primitive Induction, RPI），通过单次挖掘ReAct轨迹中的高频推理模式，将其转化为可复用的伪工具库，使新问题上的性能显著超越原始生成轨迹的Agent。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ReAct风格的LLM智能体在解决问题时经常重复相同的推理步骤，但这些模式被局限于临时的scratchpad中，无法系统性地复用，导致效率低下和性能瓶颈。

Method: 单次方法：挖掘成功ReAct轨迹 → 聚类重复推理动作 → 将高频动作转化为带自然语言文档字符串(type pseudo-tools)的紧凑库 → 标准ReAct循环在测试时组合这些基元。

Abstract: ReAct-style LLM agents often rediscover the same reasoning routines across problems, yet leave those routines trapped in transient scratchpads. We introduce Reasoning Primitive Induction, a single-pass method that mines successful ReAct traces, clusters recurrent reasoning moves, and converts the most frequent moves into a compact library of typed pseudo-tools. Each pseudo-tool is specified by a natural-language docstring interpreted by an LLM at invocation time, and a standard ReAct loop composes these primitives at test time. The central result is that induced libraries outperform the very agent that generated their traces: by +44pp on RuleArena NBA (30 -> 74), +30pp on MuSR team allocation (38 -> 68), and +22pp on NatPlan meeting planning (7 -> 29). Across five comparable subtasks spanning narrative deduction, rule application, and constraint-satisfaction planning, a single fixed configuration improves over zero-shot Chain-of-Thought on every subtask, matches or surpasses expert-authored decompositions, and outperforms AWM at lower average inference cost.

### [256] [AUDITFLOW: Executable Symbolic Environments for Structured Financial Reporting Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03031)
*Yan Wang,Xuguang Ai,Jaisal Patel,Xueqing Peng,Fengran Mo,Yupeng Cao,Haohang Li,Mingyu Cao,Lingfei Qian,Víctor Gutiérrez-Basulto*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在结构化金融审计验证中面临困难，因为正确性取决于结构化证据而非纯文本，模型需要将报告事实关联到分类概念、遍历计算或维度关系、重新计算预期值后再应用审计规则，这些步骤对纯语言模型具有挑战性。

Result: 在FinAuditing派生的FinMR样本上，AuditFlow在GPT-5.5下达到82.09%联合审计准确率，比最强基线高出14.93个百分点。去除确定性检查后准确率骤降至17.91%，表明符号环境执行了模型无法可靠替代的验证步骤。

Conclusion: 符号环境在结构化审计验证中执行了关键且不可替代的验证步骤，将自适应搜索与确定性验证分离的图基多智能体框架能有效提升审计准确性。

Abstract: Structured financial audit verification is difficult for language-model agents because correctness depends on structured evidence rather than text alone. A model must link reported facts to taxonomy concepts, traverse calculation or dimensional relations, and recompute expected values before applying an audit rule. We propose AuditFlow, a graph-grounded multi-agent framework that separates adaptive search from deterministic verification. AuditFlow builds a symbolic environment from a static US-GAAP taxonomy graph and a dynamic XBRL filing graph, and exposes it through typed tools for fact retrieval, taxonomy traversal, numerical checking, and rule evaluation. Two junior auditors inspect each case from regulatory and evidentiary views, while a senior auditor resolves disagreements and can request further investigation. The final reports are fused through evidential aggregation to produce an audit verdict, expected value, evidence trail, and trustworthiness score. On a FinAuditing-derived FinMR sample, AuditFlow reaches 82.09% joint audit accuracy under GPT-5.5, outperforming the strongest baseline by 14.93 points. Removing deterministic checks drops accuracy to 17.91%, showing that the symbolic environment performs the verification step that the model cannot reliably replace.

### [257] [Dynamic Objective Selection with Safeguards and LLM Oversight for Financial Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03704)
*Keigo Sakurai,Takahiro Ogawa,Miki Haseyama,Anjyu Anan,Kei Nakagawa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出DOSS框架，通过基于学习的动态目标函数选择器，结合置信度门控、故障安全机制和大语言模型监督，实现金融决策中目标函数的自适应切换，避免传统潜在状态估计方法的噪声和延迟问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统金融决策中固定目标函数在不同市场环境下表现欠佳，而基于潜在状态估计的机制切换方法存在噪声、延迟和高换手率等问题，需要一种更稳健的动态目标选择方案。

Method: 1) 将目标选择形式化为分类问题，从可解释的统计摘要中学习选择目标函数；2) 使用滚动窗口进行顺序更新，避免时间泄漏；3) 采用置信度感知门控机制，低置信度时回退到保守默认；4) 显式控制切换频率；5) 引入LLM作为监督组件，仅允许接受提议或覆盖为安全默认。

Result: 通过分类框架实现目标函数动态选择，结合置信度门控和切换约束提升稳定性，LLM监督层提供治理保障。

Conclusion: DOSS提供了一种无需显式潜在状态估计的动态目标选择方法，通过多层安全机制（置信度门控、频率控制、LLM监督）平衡适应性与稳定性。

Abstract: Financial decision-making tasks such as stock recommendation and portfolio allocation typically estimate future return and risk and then select trades or allocations for an investor, and the chosen optimization objective often determines realized performance. However, because market conditions evolve over time, a fixed objective can be suboptimal across regimes, while regime-switching pipelines that rely on latent regime estimates can be noisy or delayed and frequent switching can increase turnover and operational instability. In this paper, we propose DOSS (Dynamic Objective Selection with Safeguards), a learning-based selector that directly chooses the decision-relevant objective function at each time point from interpretable statistical summaries of recent returns, selecting among a small set of candidates (e.g., return-seeking, loss-averse, and risk-adjusted) without introducing intermediate regime variables. DOSS formulates objective selection as a classification problem over objectives and performs sequential updates with a rolling window to make forward-looking selections without temporal leakage, while also outputting a confidence score for each proposal. To mitigate misselection and excessive switching in deployment, DOSS applies confidence-aware gating with a fail-safe that overrides low-confidence proposals to a conservative default and enforces explicit controls tied to switching frequency. We further integrate governance by positioning a Large Language Model (LLM) as an oversight component rather than a generator of new objectives: the LLM is restricted to accept a proposed objective or override it to a predefined safe default, with deterministic rule-based constraints triggering overrides when needed.

### [259] [RelGT-AC: A Relational Graph Transformer for Autocomplete Tasks in Relational Databases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03040)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关系数据库在多个领域至关重要，但其多表、异质和时间结构使得预测性机器学习具有挑战性。Relational Deep Learning通过将数据库表示为异构图并应用GNN来解决这一问题，但自动补全任务（预测现有列值）仍需更有效的解决方案。

Method: 提出RelGT-AC方法，包含三个贡献：(1) 列掩码策略，在子图编码期间屏蔽目标列以防止平凡解；(2) 统一任务头，支持二分类、多分类和回归自动补全任务；(3) TF-IDF文本编码器，自动检测并编码自由文本列，恢复词性信号。

Result: 在3个RelBench v2数据集（rel-trial, rel-f1, rel-stack）的7个任务上，RelGT-AC在所有3个回归自动补全任务上超越GraphSAGE基线，在文本密集型任务上通过TF-IDF编码器实现高达+10 AUROC的提升。

Conclusion: RelGT-AC通过针对性设计有效提升了关系数据库自动补全任务的性能，尤其文本编码策略对富含文本数据的任务贡献显著。

Abstract: Relational databases underpin modern enterprise, scientific, and healthcare systems, yet predictive machine learning on such data remains challenging due to their multi-table, heterogeneous, and temporal structure. Relational Deep Learning (RDL) addresses this by representing databases as heterogeneous graphs and applying graph neural networks (GNNs) directly. RelBench v2 recently introduced autocomplete tasks -- a practically motivated task type where the goal is to predict an existing column value from relational context, analogous to an intelligent form-filling assistant. We propose RelGT-AC (Relational Graph Transformer for Autocomplete), extending the RelGT architecture with three targeted contributions: (1) a column masking strategy that prevents trivial solutions by masking the target column during subgraph encoding; (2) a unified task head supporting binary classification, multiclass classification, and regression autocomplete tasks within a single model; and (3) a TF-IDF text encoder that automatically detects and encodes free-text columns, recovering strong lexical signal that categorical encoders discard. Across 7 tasks spanning 3 RelBench v2 datasets (rel-trial, rel-f1, rel-stack), RelGT-AC outperforms the GraphSAGE baseline on all 3 regression autocomplete tasks and achieves up to +10 AUROC points on text-heavy eligibility tasks via the TF-IDF encoder.

### [260] [ToolGate: Token-Efficient Pre-Call Control for Tool-Augmented Vision-Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03054)
*Anjie Liu,Yan Song,Zhixun Chen,Ziqin Gong,Zhongwei Yu,Jun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ToolGate，一种轻量级外部控制器，用于在工具增强的视觉语言智能体中决定是否执行感知工具调用。研究发现基线智能体在11.8%的有益调用和9.9%的有害调用之间缺乏选择性，而ToolGate可将token成本降至ReAct基线的64-69%，同时保持甚至提升平均准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具增强的视觉语言智能体在执行每个提议的工具调用时成本高昂且不必要，现有ReAct风格的VLM智能体缺乏对工具调用是否真正有益的选择性判断能力，需要一种预调用的控制机制来避免不必要的工具执行。

Method: 提出ToolGate，一种轻量级外部控制器，从轨迹文本和简单结构特征中预测执行/跳过决策。在五个基准上评估基线智能体的调用选择性，并在两个Qwen3-VL骨干网络上测试ToolGate的效果。

Result: 基线智能体中，有益调用和有害调用比例接近（11.8% vs 9.9%），大多数调用不改变预测结果。ToolGate将token成本降至ReAct基线的64-69%，在跨领域设置中保持平均准确率，在同领域设置中进一步将平均准确率提升1.65个点。

Conclusion: 工具增强的VLM智能体不仅受益于更好的感知工具，还需要对工具输出何时值得付费进行明确的控制，即通过显式控制决定是否执行工具调用。

Abstract: Tool-augmented vision-language agents can acquire external perceptual evidence through OCR, detection, segmentation, and other tools, but executing every proposed tool call is costly and sometimes unnecessary. We study the pre-call control problem: after a ReAct-style VLM agent proposes a perceptual tool call, should the call be executed, or skipped before its output enters the context? Across five benchmarks, we find that the baseline agent exhibits poor local selectivity: helpful and harmful calls occur at similar rates (11.8% vs. 9.9%), while most calls do not change the immediate forced-answer prediction. We introduce ToolGate, a lightweight external controller that predicts execute/skip decisions from trajectory text and simple structural features. Across two Qwen3-VL backbones, ToolGate reduces token cost to 64-69% of the unrestricted ReAct baseline while preserving average accuracy in cross-domain settings. With matched-domain trajectory training on Qwen3-VL-30B, it further improves average accuracy by 1.65 points. These results show that tool-augmented VLM agents benefit not only from better perceptual tools, but also from explicit control over when tool outputs are worth paying for.

### [261] [SkillDAG: Self-Evolving Typed Skill Graphs for LLM Skill Selection at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03056)
*Tong Bai,Zhenglin Wan,Pengfei Zhou,Xingrui Yu,Wangbo Zhao,Yang You,Ivor W. Tsang*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体拥有大规模技能库时，技能之间存在依赖、冲突、特化、重复等结构性关系，而传统的枚举或嵌入相似度方法无法捕捉这种结构，导致技能选择效果不佳。

Method: SkillDAG将技能间关系建模为类型化有向图，在推理时作为智能体可调用的结构化检索接口，支持向量匹配、类型边邻居和冲突信号三种搜索方式；采用"提议-提交"协议让智能体在执行过程中注册经验验证的边，使图结构跨回合积累演化。

Result: 在ALFWorld和SkillsBench上使用MiniMax-M2.7达到67.1%成功率和27.3%奖励，超过Graph-of-Skills基线+12.8和+8.6个点；SkillsBench Ret@K从65.5提升到78.2。

Conclusion: SkillDAG的优势源于两个可隔离机制：候选排名在技能池扩大10倍时仍保持鲁棒（而固定扩散流程会退化），以及集合单调的在线编辑能扩大真实召回率而不驱逐先前命中项。

Abstract: As LLM agents adopt large skill libraries, selecting the right subset becomes a structural problem rather than a similarity-matching one: skills depend on, conflict with, specialize, or duplicate one another, a structure invisible to both full enumeration and embedding similarity. We present SkillDAG, which models inter-skill relationships as a typed directed graph and exposes it to an LLM agent as an inference-time, agent-callable structural retrieval interface, queried and evolved during execution rather than baked into a fixed retrieval pipeline: each search returns vector matches, typed-edge neighbors, and conflict signals, and a propose-then-commit protocol lets the agent register execution-backed edges so the graph accumulates structure across episodes. On ALFWorld and SkillsBench with MiniMax-M2.7, SkillDAG reaches 67.1% success and 27.3% reward, exceeding the strongest reported Graph-of-Skills baseline by +12.8 and +8.6 points; the advantage ports to gpt-5.2-codex, and intrinsic SkillsBench Ret@K rises from 65.5 to 78.2 under matched queries. These gains trace to isolable mechanisms: candidate ranking that stays robust as the pool grows 10x where a fixed seeding-diffusion pipeline degrades, and set-monotone online edits that enlarge ground-truth recall without evicting prior hits.

Method: 提出CORE框架，首先构建带有细粒度冲突因素和来源标注的冲突归因语料库(CAC)，然后基于CAC进行冲突导向的表示增强与推理，使多模态大语言模型具备显式冲突捕捉能力。

Inspired by this observation, we propose \textbf{C}onflict-\textbf{O}riented \textbf{RE}asoning (\textbf{CORE}) framework, an effective paradigm that learns to endows multimodal large language models (MLLMs) with explicit conflict-capturing capability. To this end, CORE first constructs the Conflict Attribution Corpus (CAC) with fine-grained annotations of conflict factors and sources, providing essential data support for subsequent conflict perception training. By performing conflict-oriented representation enhancement and reasoning based on CAC, CORE achieves robust and generalizable conflict detection, effectively and rapidly adapting to unseen manipulation types with a few samples or in even zero-shot settings. ### [263] [DELTAMEM: Incremental Experience Memory for LLM Agents via Residual Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03083)
*Haoran Tan,Zeyu Zhang,Zhicheng Cao,Rui Li,Xu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出DeltaMem框架，通过残差经验树结构组织记忆，将经验存储为增量变化而非独立扁平单元，解决冗余和检索冲突问题，在多个交互环境中取得更好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体将经验存储为独立扁平单元，导致大量冗余（相似经验重复存储重叠内容）和检索冲突（细微场景变化导致矛盾指导），亟需一种更高效的经验组织方式。

Method: DeltaMem构建两棵独立残差树（目标条件任务技能树+场景环境知识树），每棵树以根节点存储泛化基础经验，增量delta节点存储后续变化；检索时采用失败惩罚相似度扫描定位最佳匹配，通过根到匹配节点的链式组合重建完整经验；自主整合机制将高频路径蒸馏为新的根节点，实现树结构的自组织。

Result: 在多种交互环境中的实验表明，DeltaMem持续优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 残差经验结构能有效减少记忆冗余并缓解检索冲突，为LLM智能体的持续学习提供了更高效的记忆组织范式。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents increasingly rely on memory to learn from experiences over continual interactions. However, storing experiences as independent, flat units leads to substantial redundancy and retrieval conflicts, as similar episodes repeat overlapping content and subtle scene variations cause retrieved memories to offer contradictory guidance. To address this, we introduce residual experience, positing that newly acquired experience is often an incremental variation of existing knowledge. We propose DeltaMem, a framework that organizes experience memory into two independent residual trees, one storing goal-conditioned task experience as reusable skills and another for scene-level environment knowledge. Each tree uses a root node for generalized base experiences and incremental delta nodes for subsequent variations, allowing related experiences to share a common foundation without duplication. For retrieval, a failure-penalized similarity scan locates the best match, reconstructing the full experience via root-to-match chain composition. An autonomous consolidation mechanism distills high-frequency paths into new root nodes, enabling the trees to self-organize from general heuristics to specialized variants. Experiments across diverse interactive environments show that DeltaMem consistently outperforms existing baselines. To facilitate future research, we release the code at https://github.com/import-myself/DeltaMem.
